RACE OVERVIEW
=============
The 2024 Formula 1 Spanish Grand Prix took place on June 23, 2024, at the Circuit de Barcelona-Catalunya. Max Verstappen of Red Bull Racing secured his third straight Spanish Grand Prix victory, marking his seventh win of the 2024 season. Despite starting behind pole-sitter Lando Norris and initially losing the lead to George Russell, Verstappen quickly regained control, passing Russell on Lap 3. Norris, driving for McLaren, finished second after a strategic battle, while Lewis Hamilton of Mercedes took third place, earning his first podium finish of the season. The race also featured close battles in the midfield, including contact between the Ferraris of Charles Leclerc and Carlos Sainz Jr.


=============
